<t>CREATE TABLE city (
    city_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    city_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    population INT
);


CREATE TABLE sensors (
    sensor_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    sensor_type VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    city_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (city_id) REFERENCES city(city_id)
);


CREATE TABLE events (
    event_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    event_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    event_date DATE,
    city_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (city_id) REFERENCES city(city_id)
);


CREATE TABLE weather (
    weather_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    temperature INT,
    humidity FLOAT,
    city_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (city_id) REFERENCES city(city_id)
);
</t><s>UPDATE city SET population = 100000 WHERE city_id = 1;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE city (

    population INT

CREATE TABLE devices (device_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, device_name STRING, user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id), location STRING)

CREATE TABLE events (event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, event_name STRING, sensor_id UUID REFERENCES sensors(sensor_id), event_type STRING)

CREATE TABLE sensors (sensor_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, sensor_type STRING, device_id UUID REFERENCES devices(device_id), status STRING)</t><s>update sensors set status = 'active' where sensor_id = 'a64b8a08-09c6-4c23-87f0-843079d72710';</s>
